<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:компонента.html>компоне́нта</a> (12972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:компромат.html>компрома́т</a> (18150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компрометирующий.html>компромети́рующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komprometírujuščij materiál</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромат.html>компрома́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kompromát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромат.html>компрома́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромат.html>компрома́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромат.html>компрома́тов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:компрометировать.html>компромети́ровать</a> (16722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">compromettre</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***компромисс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сс</a> (8884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1718. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">comprōmissum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kompromíss</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́ссов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компромиссный.html>компроми́ссный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>compromise, trade-off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сс</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí na <b>kompromíss</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to compromise, make a compromise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сс</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s trudóm najtí <b>kompromíss</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to find the compromise with difficulty</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kompʹjútɛr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́теры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́теров</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютерный.html>компью́терный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kompʹjútɛrnyj</span>)

***комсомол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́л</a> (5195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komsomól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́лов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комсомольский.html>комсомо́льский</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">acronym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коммунистический.html>коммунисти́ческий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодежь.html>молодёжи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kommunistíčeskij sojúz molodjóži</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Communist Union of Youth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: Komsomol, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Young_Communist_League" class="extiw" title="w:Young Communist League">Young Communist League</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комфортабельный.html>комфорта́бельный</a> (16760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">confortable</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word may be borrowed from either French or English; the accent matches French, but the spelling matches English.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комфортабельный.html>комфорта́бельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komfortábelʹnyj</span>)
</p>

***кон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>кон</a> (10314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">конъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">limit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beginning; end</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>кон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>ко́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>коны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>коно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>gambling</i> bank, kitty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>кон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">postávitʹ na kon</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to place one's stake, to put one's money in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>game, round</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конечный.html>коне́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konéčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испокон.html>испоко́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ispokón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">споко́н</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spokón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***конвейер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йер</a> (11062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">conveyor</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konvéjer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йеров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conveyor, production line</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conveyor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a method of interrogation in which investigators conduct the questioning in round-the-clock shifts, in order to induce sleep deprivation in the subject</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1975</b>,  Юрий Осипович Домбровский (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yury_Dombrovsky" class="extiw" title="w:Yury Dombrovsky">Yury Osipovich Dombrovsky</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:факультет.html>Факульте́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ненужный.html>нену́жных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>вещей</a></cite>  | <cite>The Faculty of Useless Knowledge</cite> | , part 2, chapter 5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>Про</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будильник.html>буди́льников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказывать.html>расска́зывал</a> буддо́. <a href = vnd.unilang:будильник.html>буди́льники</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курсант.html>курса́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:юридический.html>юриди́ческой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лы</a> НКВД, <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отбывать.html>отбыва́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:практика.html>пра́ктику</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ние</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:конвейер.html>конве́йере</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:следствие.html>сле́дствие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:непрерывно.html>непреры́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сутки.html>су́ток</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>то́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pro budílʹnikov jemú rasskázyval Buddó. Budílʹniki — éto kursánty výsšej juridíčeskoj škóly NKVD, zdesʹ oní otbyvájut práktiku. Glávnoje ix naznačénije — sidétʹ na <b>konvéjere</b>. Slédstvije dólžno idtí neprerývno néskolʹko sútok, ináče tólku ne búdet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Buddo had told him about the alarm clocks. Alarm clocks were cadets at the NKVD higher law school; here they were serving their internship. Their main assignment was to sit on the <b>conveyor</b>. An investigation was supposed to go on uninterruptedly for several days and nights, otherwise there would be no use in it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">convoy</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвой.html>конво́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konvój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвой.html>конво́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвой.html>конво́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвой.html>конво́ев</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвой.html>конво́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konvój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конвойный.html>конво́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konvójnyj</span>)

***кондитер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кондитер.html>конди́тер</a> (29396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Konditer</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Konditor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">condītor</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондитер.html>конди́тер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kondíter</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондитер.html>конди́тера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондитер.html>конди́теры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондитер.html>конди́теров</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">конди́терша</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>confectioner, pastry cook</li>
<li>confectionery owner</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small restaurant owner</li></ol>

***кондиция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кондиция.html>конди́ция</a> (27091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондиция.html>конди́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kondícija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондиция.html>конди́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондиция.html>конди́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондиция.html>конди́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>state, condition</li></ol>
